// monkey patch createElement so that when 3rd parties add new scripts
// to the document we can check them against our blacklist before the
// script source is fetched
var createElementBackup = document.createElement;
document.createElement = function () {
  var element = createElementBackup.apply(document, arguments);
  if (arguments[0].toLowerCase() !== 'script') {
    return element;
  }
  var originalSetAttribute = element.setAttribute.bind(element);

  // first use properties for src and type so we can override
  // document.createElement('script').src = 'bad.url.com'
  Object.defineProperties(element, {
    'src': {
      get: function () {
        return element.getAttribute('src');
      },
      set: function (value) {
        if (isBlacklisted(value)) {
          originalSetAttribute('type', 'javascript/blocked');
        }
        originalSetAttribute('src', value);
        return true;
      }
    },
    'type': {
      get: function () {
        return element.getAttribute('type');
      },
      set: function (value) {
        var type = isBlacklisted(element.src)
          ? 'javascript/blocked'
          : value;
        originalSetAttribute('type', type);
        return true;
      }
    }
  });

  // also need to monkey patch the element's setAttribute because
  // script.setAttribute('src', 'bad.url.com');
  // bypasses our src setter function above
  element.setAttribute = function (name, value) {
    if (name === 'src' || name === 'type') {
      element[name] = value;
    } else {
      HTMLScriptElement.prototype.setAttribute.call(element, name, value);
    }
  };

  return element;
};

function isBlacklisted(src) {
  var blacklist = window && window._wml &&
    window._wml.config &&
    window._wml.config.ccm &&
    window._wml.config.ccm.blacklist;
  return !!src && containsMatchingValue(blacklist, src);
}

function containsMatchingValue(expressions = {}, source) {
  return Object.keys(expressions).some(function (key) {
    var expression = expressions[key];
    if (typeof expression === 'string' && expression.length) {
      return new RegExp(expressions[key]).test(source);
    }
    return false;
  });
};
